# mapping
# ng/ñ -> r
# oe/ö -> y
# eo/ö -> y
# yu/ü -> v
# aa/ā -> r
# gw/ģ -> x
# kw/ķ -> q
# j/y  -> j

# keyboard layout
# ķ w e ñ/ā t ö u i o p
# a s d f   g h y k l
# z ģ c ü   b n m
